# Tags:
# rank_headgear: any headgear that signifies a certain title. crowns, pope hat etc.



headgear = {
	# interface_position = 1
	usage = game
	selection_behavior = weighted_random
	
	no_hat = {
		usage = game 
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
		
				gene = headgear
				template = no_headgear
				value = 0
			}
		}
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 1000
				AND = {
					# Deliberately not the "fully naked" one since dropping your crown's intended even if nudity is disabled
					should_be_naked_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					is_adult = no
					highest_held_title_tier >= tier_duchy # Should wear ducal or royal crown instead.
					AND = {
						religion = religion:christianity_religion
						faith.religious_head = this
					}
				}
			}
			# Refuses to wear a crown due to HighGod.
			modifier = {
				add = 110
				has_character_modifier = fp1_abased_before_highgod_modifier
			}
		}
	}

## So that the Prophet Muhammad does not have a portrait ## 

	no_portrait = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add				
				gene = headgear
				template = no_headgear
				value = 0.5
			}
		}
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 200
				this = character:33922
			}
		}
	}

	no_headgear = {

		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear
				template = no_headgear
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		
		weight = {
			## No headgear for children under 16 ## 
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				age < 16
			}
			# No headgear for characters with an active Vow of Poverty
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				has_character_modifier = vow_of_poverty_modifier
				# Should still wear armor when going to war
				NOT = { portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes }
			}
		}
	}



	vanity_no_headgear = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear
				template = no_headgear
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	

		## No headgear for vanity characters with the no_headgear flag, unless they are dukes or higher
		weight = {  
			base = 0
            modifier = {
                add = 200
                has_character_flag = no_headgear
                highest_held_title_tier < tier_duchy
            }
		}
	}


## DDE HRE ##

## Western ##

	dde_hre_commoners = {

		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear
				template = dde_hre_common
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				highest_held_title_tier < tier_county
				NOR = {
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						primary_spouse = {
							highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_government = republic_government
						primary_title.tier > 1
					}
					AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
				}
				portrait_dde_hre_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
		###High medieval headgears		
				OR = {
				EPE_culture_era_high_medieval_trigger = yes	##High to late era			
				current_date >= 1026.1.1	##early era				
				}									
			}
		}
	}
	
	hre_mayors = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear
				template = dde_hre_common

			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 60
				highest_held_title_tier < tier_county
				has_government = republic_government
				portrait_dde_hre_clothing_trigger = yes
		###High medieval headgears		
				OR = {
				EPE_culture_era_high_medieval_trigger = yes	##High to late era			
				current_date >= 1026.1.1	##early era				
				}				
									
			}
		}
	}	

	dde_hre_low_nobles = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear
				template = dde_hre_nobility
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				NAND = {
					has_trait = peasant_leader
					OR = {
						is_ruler = no
						is_leading_faction_type = peasant_faction
						AND = {
							is_ruler = yes
							is_landed = no
							OR = {
								has_government = feudal_government
								has_government = clan_government
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					AND = {
						highest_held_title_tier = tier_county
						NOR = {
							# has_dynasty = no
							AND = {
								has_government = republic_government
								primary_title.tier > 1
							}
							AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
						}
						portrait_dde_hre_clothing_trigger = yes
		###High medieval headgears		
				OR = {
				EPE_culture_era_high_medieval_trigger = yes	##High to late era			
				current_date >= 1026.1.1	##early era				
				}				
										
					}
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						OR = {
							is_ruler = no
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_barony
						}
						primary_spouse = {
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_county
							NOR = {
								# has_dynasty = no
								AND = {
									has_government = republic_government
									primary_title.tier > 1
								}
								AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
							}
							portrait_dde_hre_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
		###High medieval headgears		
				OR = {
				EPE_culture_era_high_medieval_trigger = yes	##High to late era			
				current_date >= 1026.1.1	##early era				
				}				
											
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	dde_hre_high_nobles = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear
				template = dde_hre_high_nobility
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				NAND = {
					has_trait = peasant_leader
					OR = {
						is_ruler = no
						is_leading_faction_type = peasant_faction
						AND = {
							is_ruler = yes
							is_landed = no
							OR = {
								has_government = feudal_government

							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_duchy
							AND = {
								has_government = republic_government
								primary_title.tier > 2
							}
							AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
						}
						NOT = { AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = mercenary_government  } } # Blocked for mercenaries
						portrait_dde_hre_clothing_trigger = yes
		###High medieval headgears		
				OR = {
				EPE_culture_era_high_medieval_trigger = yes	##High to late era			
				current_date >= 1026.1.1	##early era				
				}				
											
					}
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						OR = {
							is_ruler = no
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_barony
						}
						primary_spouse = {
							OR = {
								highest_held_title_tier = tier_duchy
								AND = {
									has_government = republic_government
									primary_title.tier > 2
								}
								AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
							}
							portrait_dde_hre_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
		###High medieval headgears

				current_date >= 1026.1.1	##early era				
				}				
												
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	# Reichskrone
	hre_imperial = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear
				template = dde_hre_imperial
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 101 # always pick the HRE crown over the western one
				has_primary_title = title:e_hre
			}
		}
	}


	
	
	dde_hre_war = {
		dna_modifiers = {
		
			morph = {
				mode = add
				
				gene = gene_bs_ear_outward
				template = ear_outward_neg
				value = 1.0
			}	
		
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear
				template = dde_hre_war
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 101
				portrait_wear_helmet_trigger = yes
				portrait_dde_hre_clothing_trigger = yes
				EPE_armor_era_high_medieval_trigger = yes					
				NOR = {
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        has_government = holy_order_government
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        is_landed = no
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        exists = liege
				        liege = {
				            has_government = holy_order_government
				        }
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        OR = {
				            any_character_war = {
				                OR = {
				                    using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                    using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                }
				                is_attacker = prev
				            }
				            any_liege_or_above = {
				                faith = prev.faith
				                any_character_war = {
				                    OR = {
				                        using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                        using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                    }
				                    is_attacker = prev
				                }
				            }
				        }
				    }
				}
			}
		}
	}

								AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
							}
							NOT = { AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = mercenary_government  } } # Blocked for mercenaries
							NOT = { has_government = republic_government }
							portrait_western_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
		###High medieval headgears		
				OR = {
				EPE_culture_era_high_medieval_trigger = yes	##High to late era			
				current_date >= 1026.1.1	##early era				
				}							
						}
					}
				}

			}
		}
	}


	western_war = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			morph = {
				mode = add
				
				gene = gene_bs_ear_outward
				template = ear_outward_neg
				value = 1.0
			}			
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear
				template = western_war
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				portrait_wear_helmet_trigger = yes
				portrait_western_clothing_trigger = yes
				EPE_armor_era_high_medieval_trigger = yes					
				NOR = {
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        has_government = holy_order_government
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        is_landed = no
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        exists = liege
				        liege = {
				            has_government = holy_order_government
				        }
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        OR = {
				            any_character_war = {
				                OR = {
				                    using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                    using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                }
				                is_attacker = prev
				            }
				            any_liege_or_above = {
				                faith = prev.faith
				                any_character_war = {
				                    OR = {
				                        using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                        using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                    }
				                    is_attacker = prev
				                }
				            }
				        }
				    }
				}
			}
		}

## Byzantine ##


	byzantine_commoners = {

		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear
				template = byzantine_common
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				highest_held_title_tier < tier_county
				NOR = {
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						primary_spouse = {
							highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_government = republic_government
						primary_title.tier > 1
					}
					AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
				}
				portrait_byzantine_clothing_trigger = yes
			}
		}
	}

	byzantine_low_nobles = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear
				template = byzantine_nobility
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				NAND = {
					has_trait = peasant_leader
					OR = {
						is_ruler = no
						is_leading_faction_type = peasant_faction
						AND = {
							is_ruler = yes
							is_landed = no
							OR = {
								has_government = feudal_government
								has_government = clan_government
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					AND = {
						highest_held_title_tier = tier_county
						NOR = {
							# has_dynasty = no
							AND = {
								has_government = republic_government
								primary_title.tier > 1
							}
							AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
						}
						portrait_byzantine_clothing_trigger = yes
					}
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						OR = {
							is_ruler = no
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_barony
						}
						primary_spouse = {
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_county
							NOR = {
								# has_dynasty = no
								AND = {
									has_government = republic_government
									primary_title.tier > 1
								}
								AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
							}
							portrait_byzantine_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	byzantine_high_nobles = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear
				template = byzantine_high_nobility
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				NAND = {
					has_trait = peasant_leader
					OR = {
						is_ruler = no
						is_leading_faction_type = peasant_faction
						AND = {
							is_ruler = yes
							is_landed = no
							OR = {
								has_government = feudal_government
								has_government = clan_government
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_duchy
							AND = {
								has_government = republic_government
								primary_title.tier > 2
							}
							AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
						}
						NOT = { AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = mercenary_government  } } # Blocked for mercenaries
						portrait_byzantine_clothing_trigger = yes
					}
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						OR = {
							is_ruler = no
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_barony
						}
						primary_spouse = {
							OR = {
								highest_held_title_tier = tier_duchy
								AND = {
									has_government = republic_government
									primary_title.tier > 2
								}
								AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
							}
							portrait_byzantine_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

					has_trait = peasant_leader
					OR = {
						is_ruler = no
						is_leading_faction_type = peasant_faction
						AND = {
							is_ruler = yes
							is_landed = no
							OR = {
								has_government = feudal_government
								has_government = clan_government
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_empire
							AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
						}
						NOT = { AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = mercenary_government  } } # Blocked for mercenaries
						NOT = { has_government = republic_government }
				        portrait_byzantine_clothing_trigger = yes
					}
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						OR = {
							is_ruler = no
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_barony
						}
						primary_spouse = {
							OR = {
								highest_held_title_tier = tier_empire
								AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
							}
							NOT = { AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = mercenary_government  } } # Blocked for mercenaries
							NOT = { has_government = republic_government }
			            	portrait_byzantine_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
						}
					}
				}

			}
		}
	}	
	
	byzantine_war = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			morph = {
				mode = add
				
				gene = gene_bs_ear_outward
				template = ear_outward_neg
				value = 1.0
			}		
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear
				template = byzantine_war
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 101 # larger than the western war headgear
				portrait_wear_helmet_trigger = yes
				portrait_byzantine_clothing_trigger = yes
				
				NOR = {
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        has_government = holy_order_government
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        is_landed = no
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        exists = liege
				        liege = {
				            has_government = holy_order_government
				        }
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        OR = {
				            any_character_war = {
				                OR = {
				                    using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                    using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                }
				                is_attacker = prev
				            }
				            any_liege_or_above = {
				                faith = prev.faith
				                any_character_war = {
				                    OR = {
				                        using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                        using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                    }
				                    is_attacker = prev
				                }
				            }
				        }
				    }
				}
			}
		}
	}	

## INDIAN ##

	indian_commoners = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear
				template = indian_common
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 80
				has_trait = peasant_leader
				OR = {
					is_ruler = no
					is_leading_faction_type = peasant_faction
					AND = {
						is_ruler = yes
						is_landed = no
						OR = {
							has_government = feudal_government
							has_government = clan_government
						}
					}
				}
				portrait_indian_clothing_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				highest_held_title_tier < tier_county
				NOR = {
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						primary_spouse = {
							highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_government = republic_government
						primary_title.tier > 1
					}
					AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
				}
				portrait_indian_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
			}
		}
	}

							highest_held_title_tier = tier_empire
							AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
						}
						NOT = { AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = mercenary_government  } } # Blocked for mercenaries
						NOT = { has_government = republic_government }
				OR = {
					portrait_mena_clothing_trigger = yes
								AND = {
				    portrait_iberia_muslim_clothing_trigger = yes	
						portrait_iberia_muslim_trigger = yes				
								}							
								AND = {
					portrait_dde_abbasid_clothing_trigger = yes	
                NOT = { portrait_dde_abbasid_flavor_dlc_trigger = yes } 	
				EPE_culture_era_high_medieval_trigger = yes					
								}					
				}	
					}
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						OR = {
							is_ruler = no
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_barony
						}
						primary_spouse = {
							OR = {
								highest_held_title_tier = tier_empire
								AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
							}
							NOT = { AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = mercenary_government  } } # Blocked for mercenaries
							NOT = { has_government = republic_government }
				OR = {
					portrait_mena_clothing_trigger = yes
								AND = {
					portrait_iberia_muslim_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes	
						portrait_iberia_muslim_trigger = yes						
								}						
								AND = {
					portrait_dde_abbasid_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes	
                NOT = { portrait_dde_abbasid_flavor_dlc_trigger = yes } 	
				EPE_culture_era_high_medieval_trigger = yes					
								}					
				}	
						}
					}
				}

			}
		}
	}
	

	mena_war = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			morph = {
				mode = add
				
				gene = gene_bs_ear_outward
				template = ear_outward_neg
				value = 1.0
			}		
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear
				template = mena_war
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 101
				portrait_wear_helmet_trigger = yes
				OR = {
					portrait_mena_clothing_trigger = yes
								AND = {
				    portrait_iberia_muslim_clothing_trigger = yes	
						portrait_iberia_muslim_trigger = yes				
								}						
								AND = {
					portrait_dde_abbasid_clothing_trigger = yes	
                NOT = { portrait_dde_abbasid_flavor_dlc_trigger = yes } 	
				EPE_culture_era_high_medieval_trigger = yes					
								}					
				}	
				
				NOR = {
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        has_government = holy_order_government
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        is_landed = no
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        exists = liege
				        liege = {
				            has_government = holy_order_government
				        }
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        OR = {
				            any_character_war = {
				                OR = {
				                    using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                    using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                }
				                is_attacker = prev
				            }
				            any_liege_or_above = {
				                faith = prev.faith
				                any_character_war = {
				                    OR = {
				                        using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                        using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                    }
				                    is_attacker = prev
				                }
				            }
				        }
				    }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	early_middle_ages_sunni_caliph = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear
				template = early_abbasid_caliph
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
			
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 1000
				NAND = {
					has_trait = peasant_leader
					OR = {
						is_ruler = no
						is_leading_faction_type = peasant_faction
						AND = {
							is_ruler = yes
							is_landed = no
							OR = {
								has_government = feudal_government
								has_government = clan_government
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							has_title = title:d_sunni

						}
						NOT = { AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = mercenary_government  } } # Blocked for mercenaries
						NOT = { has_government = republic_government }
				        EPE_culture_era_early_medieval_trigger = yes	
					}
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						OR = {
							is_ruler = no
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_barony
						}
						primary_spouse = {
							OR = {
								has_title = title:d_sunni

							}
							NOT = { AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = mercenary_government  } } # Blocked for mercenaries
							NOT = { has_government = republic_government }
			            	EPE_culture_era_early_medieval_trigger = yes

					}
				}

		}

	dde_abbasid_war = {
	
		dna_modifiers = {
			morph = {
				mode = add

				template = ear_outward_neg
				value = 1.0
			}

			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0

				add = 101 # slightly higher than mena
				OR = { # This helmet is really fancy & gilded - it's nothing for commoners. We allow Dukes+ to use it sometimes, just because it suits them!
					AND = {
						has_council_position = councillor_marshal
						OR = {
							is_landed = no
							primary_title.tier >= tier_duchy
						}
					}
					AND = {
						is_commanding_army = yes
						AND = {
							exists = primary_title
							primary_title.tier >= tier_duchy
						}
					}
				}
				portrait_dde_abbasid_clothing_trigger = yes
				EPE_culture_era_early_medieval_trigger = yes	
				portrait_dde_abbasid_flavor_dlc_trigger = yes	
				
				NOR = {
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        has_government = holy_order_government
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        is_landed = no
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        exists = liege
				        liege = {
				            has_government = holy_order_government
				        }
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        OR = {
				            any_character_war = {
				                OR = {
				                    using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                    using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                }
				                is_attacker = prev
				            }
				            any_liege_or_above = {
				                faith = prev.faith
				                any_character_war = {
				                    OR = {
				                        using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                        using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                    }
				                    is_attacker = prev
				                }
				            }
				        }
				    }
					AND = {

						OR = {
							is_ruler = no
							is_leading_faction_type = peasant_faction
							AND = {
								is_ruler = yes
								is_landed = no

								primary_title.tier > 2
							}
							AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
						}
						NOT = { AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = mercenary_government  } } # Blocked for mercenaries
						portrait_steppe_clothing_trigger = yes
					}
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						OR = {
							is_ruler = no
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_barony
						}
						primary_spouse = {
							OR = {
								highest_held_title_tier = tier_duchy
								AND = {
									has_government = republic_government
									primary_title.tier > 2
								}
								AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
							}
							portrait_steppe_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
						}
					}
				}

			}
		}
	}

	steppe_war = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			morph = {
				mode = add
				
				gene = gene_bs_ear_outward
				template = ear_outward_neg
				value = 1.0
			}		
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear
				template = steppe_war
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				portrait_wear_helmet_trigger = yes
				portrait_steppe_clothing_trigger = yes
				
				NOR = {
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        has_government = holy_order_government
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        is_landed = no
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        exists = liege
				        liege = {
				            has_government = holy_order_government
				        }
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        OR = {
				            any_character_war = {
				                OR = {
				                    using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                    using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                }
				                is_attacker = prev
				            }
				            any_liege_or_above = {
				                faith = prev.faith
				                any_character_war = {
				                    OR = {
				                        using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                        using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                    }
				                    is_attacker = prev
				                }
				            }
				        }
				    }
				}
			}

## Northern Pagans ##

	northern_commoners = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear
				template = northern_common
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 70
				has_trait = peasant_leader
				OR = {
					is_ruler = no
					is_leading_faction_type = peasant_faction
					AND = {
						is_ruler = yes
						is_landed = no
						OR = {
							has_government = feudal_government
							has_government = clan_government
						}
					}
				}
						OR = {
							portrait_northern_clothing_trigger = yes
							portrait_gaelic_clothing_trigger = yes	

								AND = {
					portrait_balto_finnic_clothing_trigger = yes	
                NOT = { portrait_norse_flavor_dlc_trigger = yes } 					
								}								
						}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				highest_held_title_tier < tier_county
				NOR = {
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						primary_spouse = {
							highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_government = republic_government
						primary_title.tier > 1
					}
					AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
				}
						OR = {
							portrait_northern_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
							portrait_gaelic_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes	

								AND = {
					portrait_balto_finnic_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes	
                NOT = { portrait_norse_flavor_dlc_trigger = yes } 					
								}								
						}
			}
		}
	}

						has_government = republic_government
						primary_title.tier > 1
					}

				}

			}
		}
	}

									primary_title.tier > 1

	religious_orthodox_devoted = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear_2
				template = religious_orthodox_devoted
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
			morph = {
				mode = add
				gene = gene_bs_ear_outward
				template = ear_outward_neg
				value = 1.0
			}
		}
		outfit_tags = { monk_outfit }
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 101
				is_male = yes
				OR = {
					has_trait = devoted
					AND = {
						faith = {
							has_doctrine_parameter = vows_of_poverty_active
						}
						OR = {
							AND = {
								has_council_position = councillor_court_chaplain
								faith = {
									has_doctrine = doctrine_theocracy_lay_clergy
								}
							}
							is_theocratic_lessee = yes
							AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					faith = faith:orthodox
					faith = faith:armenian_apostolic
					faith = faith:coptic
					faith = faith:messalian
					faith = faith:bogomilist
					faith = faith:paulician
					faith = faith:nestorian
				}
			}
		}
	}

	        base = 0

				OR = {
					has_character_flag = need_priest_outfit
					is_theocratic_lessee = yes
					AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
				}
				OR = {
					faith = faith:orthodox
					faith = faith:armenian_apostolic
					faith = faith:coptic
					faith = faith:messalian
					faith = faith:bogomilist
					faith = faith:paulician
					faith = faith:nestorian
				}
				NAND = {	
					is_ruler = yes
					primary_title = {
						exists = controlled_faith
						controlled_faith = faith:orthodox
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					faith = {

					}
				}

	    }
	}

	        	OR = {
					portrait_western_clothing_trigger = yes
					portrait_western_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
				}
	        	OR = {
	        		AND = {
	        			is_lowborn = no
						is_female = yes
	        		}
	        		AND = {
						has_government = republic_government

	        		}
	        	}
	        }

## China ##

	chinese_commoners = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear_2
				template = chinese_common
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		    weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 80
				has_trait = peasant_leader
				OR = {
					is_ruler = no
					is_leading_faction_type = peasant_faction
					AND = {
						is_ruler = yes
						is_landed = no
						OR = {
							has_government = feudal_government
							has_government = clan_government
						}
					}
				}
				portrait_han_clothing_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				highest_held_title_tier < tier_county
				NOR = {
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						primary_spouse = {
						highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
						}
					}
					has_government = republic_government
					AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
				}
				portrait_han_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
			}
		}
	}

									primary_title.tier > 1

		dna_modifiers = {

				mode = add
				
				gene = gene_bs_ear_outward
				template = ear_outward_neg
				value = 1.0
			}		
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear_2
				template = chinese_war
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				portrait_wear_helmet_trigger = yes
				portrait_han_clothing_trigger = yes
				
				NOR = {
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        has_government = holy_order_government
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        is_landed = no
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        exists = liege
				        liege = {
				            has_government = holy_order_government
				        }
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        OR = {
				            any_character_war = {
				                OR = {
				                    using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                    using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                }
				                is_attacker = prev
				            }
				            any_liege_or_above = {
				                faith = prev.faith
				                any_character_war = {
				                    OR = {
				                        using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                        using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                    }
				                    is_attacker = prev
				                }
				            }
				        }
				    }
				}
			}
		}

							AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
						}
						portrait_central_african_clothing_trigger = yes
					}
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						OR = {
							is_ruler = no
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_barony
						}
						primary_spouse = {
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_county
							NOR = {
								# has_dynasty = no
								AND = {
									has_government = republic_government
									primary_title.tier > 1
								}
								AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
							}
							portrait_central_african_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

							is_ruler = no

							OR = {

	central_african_war = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			morph = {
				mode = add
				
				gene = gene_bs_ear_outward
				template = ear_outward_neg
				value = 1.0
			}		
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear_2
				template = central_african_war
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				portrait_wear_helmet_trigger = yes
				portrait_central_african_clothing_trigger = yes
				
				NOR = {
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        has_government = holy_order_government
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        is_landed = no
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        exists = liege
				        liege = {
				            has_government = holy_order_government
				        }
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        OR = {
				            any_character_war = {
				                OR = {
				                    using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                    using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                }
				                is_attacker = prev
				            }
				            any_liege_or_above = {
				                faith = prev.faith
				                any_character_war = {
				                    OR = {
				                        using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                        using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                    }
				                    is_attacker = prev
				                }
				            }
				        }
				    }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	
## Iranian ##

	iranian_commoners = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear
				template = iranian_common
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 80
				has_trait = peasant_leader
				OR = {
					is_ruler = no
					is_leading_faction_type = peasant_faction
					AND = {
						is_ruler = yes
						is_landed = no
						OR = {
							has_government = feudal_government
							has_government = clan_government
						}
					}
				}
				portrait_iranian_clothing_trigger = yes
				EPE_culture_era_high_medieval_trigger = yes	
				portrait_islamic_iranian_trigger = yes				
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				highest_held_title_tier < tier_county
				NOR = {
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						primary_spouse = {
							highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_government = republic_government
						primary_title.tier > 1
					}
					AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
				}
				portrait_iranian_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
				EPE_culture_era_high_medieval_trigger = yes	
				portrait_islamic_iranian_trigger = yes				
			}
		}
	}

					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						OR = {
							is_ruler = no
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_barony
						}
						primary_spouse = {
							OR = {
								highest_held_title_tier = tier_duchy
								AND = {
									has_government = republic_government
									primary_title.tier > 2
								}
								AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
							}
							portrait_turkish_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	turkish_war = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			morph = {
				mode = add
				
				gene = gene_bs_ear_outward
				template = ear_outward_neg
				value = 1.0
			}		
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear
				template = turkish_war
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				portrait_wear_helmet_trigger = yes
				portrait_turkish_clothing_trigger = yes
				
				NOR = {
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        has_government = holy_order_government
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        is_landed = no
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        exists = liege
				        liege = {
				            has_government = holy_order_government
				        }
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        OR = {
				            any_character_war = {
				                OR = {
				                    using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                    using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                }
				                is_attacker = prev
				            }
				            any_liege_or_above = {
				                faith = prev.faith
				                any_character_war = {
				                    OR = {
				                        using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                        using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                    }
				                    is_attacker = prev
				                }
				            }
				        }
				    }
				}
			}
		}
	}		
	
	
## south_south_indian ##

	south_indian_commoners = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear
				template = south_indian_common
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 80
				has_trait = peasant_leader
				OR = {
					is_ruler = no
					is_leading_faction_type = peasant_faction
					AND = {
						is_ruler = yes
						is_landed = no
						OR = {
							has_government = feudal_government
							has_government = clan_government
						}
					}
				}
				portrait_south_indian_clothing_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				highest_held_title_tier < tier_county
				NOR = {
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						primary_spouse = {
							highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_government = republic_government
						primary_title.tier > 1
					}
					AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
				}
				portrait_south_indian_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
			}
		}
	}

## french ##

	french_commoners = {

		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear
				template = french_common
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				highest_held_title_tier < tier_county
				NOR = {
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						primary_spouse = {
							highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_government = republic_government
						primary_title.tier > 1
					}
					AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
				}
		###High medieval headgears		
				OR = {
				EPE_culture_era_high_medieval_trigger = yes	##High to late era			
				current_date >= 1026.1.1	##early era				
				}				
							
				portrait_french_clothing_trigger = yes
			}
		}
	}

				EPE_culture_era_high_medieval_trigger = yes	##High to late era			
				current_date >= 1026.1.1	##early era

							portrait_french_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes

	french_imperial = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear
				template = french_imperial
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				NAND = {
					has_trait = peasant_leader
					OR = {
						is_ruler = no
						is_leading_faction_type = peasant_faction
						AND = {
							is_ruler = yes
							is_landed = no
							OR = {
								has_government = feudal_government
								has_government = clan_government
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_empire
							AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
						}
						NOT = { AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = mercenary_government  } } # Blocked for mercenaries
						NOT = { has_government = republic_government }
		###High medieval headgears		
				OR = {
				EPE_culture_era_high_medieval_trigger = yes	##High to late era			
				current_date >= 1026.1.1	##early era				
				}				
											
				        portrait_french_clothing_trigger = yes
					}
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						OR = {
							is_ruler = no
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_barony
						}
						primary_spouse = {
							OR = {
								highest_held_title_tier = tier_empire
								AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
							}
							NOT = { AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = mercenary_government  } } # Blocked for mercenaries
							NOT = { has_government = republic_government }
		###High medieval headgears		
				OR = {
				EPE_culture_era_high_medieval_trigger = yes	##High to late era			
				current_date >= 1026.1.1	##early era				
				}				
												
			            	portrait_french_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
						}
					}
				}

			}
		}

	french_war = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			morph = {
				mode = add
				
				gene = gene_bs_ear_outward
				template = ear_outward_neg
				value = 1.0
			}		
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear
				template = french_war
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 101 # larger than the western war headgear
				portrait_wear_helmet_trigger = yes
				portrait_french_clothing_trigger = yes
				EPE_armor_era_high_medieval_trigger = yes				
				
				NOR = {
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        has_government = holy_order_government
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        is_landed = no
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        exists = liege
				        liege = {
				            has_government = holy_order_government
				        }
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        OR = {
				            any_character_war = {
				                OR = {
				                    using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                    using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                }
				                is_attacker = prev
				            }
				            any_liege_or_above = {
				                faith = prev.faith
				                any_character_war = {
				                    OR = {
				                        using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                        using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                    }
				                    is_attacker = prev
				                }
				            }
				        }
				    }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	french_war_closed = {
		dna_modifiers = {
		
			morph = {
				mode = add
				
				gene = gene_bs_ear_outward
				template = ear_outward_neg
				value = 1.0
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify
				gene = gene_chin_forward
				template = chin_forward_neg
				value = -1.0
		
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify
				gene = gene_jaw_forward
				template = jaw_forward_pos
				value = -1.0
			}			
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply				
				gene = gene_bs_nose_forward
				template = nose_forward_neg				
				value = 1.0
			}		
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear
				template = french_war_closed
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 101
				NOT = { is_female = yes }				
				portrait_wear_helmet_trigger = yes
				EPE_innovation_knighthood_trigger = yes	
				#NOT = { has_game_rule = never_epe_fullplate_helmets }	
				NOT = { has_game_rule = never_epe_fullface_helmets }					
                OR = {
                    portrait_western_clothing_trigger = yes
                    portrait_french_clothing_trigger = yes
								AND = {
				    portrait_iberia_clothing_trigger = yes	
						portrait_iberia_trigger = yes				
								}	
                    portrait_dde_hre_clothing_trigger = yes	
				    portrait_anglo_saxon_clothing_trigger = yes		
                    portrait_italian_clothing_trigger = yes	
                    portrait_german_clothing_trigger = yes						
                }
				
				NOR = {
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        has_government = holy_order_government
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        is_landed = no
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        exists = liege
				        liege = {
				            has_government = holy_order_government
				        }
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        OR = {
				            any_character_war = {
				                OR = {
				                    using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                    using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                }
				                is_attacker = prev
				            }
				            any_liege_or_above = {
				                faith = prev.faith
				                any_character_war = {
				                    OR = {
				                        using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                        using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                    }
				                    is_attacker = prev
				                }
				            }
				        }
				    }
				}
			}
		}
	}

				NOR = {
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						primary_spouse = {
							highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_government = republic_government
						primary_title.tier > 1
					}
					AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
				}
				portrait_italian_clothing_trigger = yes
		###High medieval headgears		
				OR = {
				EPE_culture_era_high_medieval_trigger = yes	##High to late era			
				current_date >= 1026.1.1	##early era				
				}				
			}
		}
	}

				gene = gene_bs_ear_outward
				template = ear_outward_neg
				value = 1.0
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify
				gene = gene_chin_forward
				template = chin_forward_neg
				value = -1.0
		
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify
				gene = gene_jaw_forward
				template = jaw_forward_pos
				value = -1.0
			}			
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply				
				gene = gene_bs_nose_forward
				template = nose_forward_neg				
				value = 1.0
			}		
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear
				template = italian_war_closed
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 101
				NOT = { is_female = yes }				
				portrait_wear_helmet_trigger = yes
				EPE_armor_era_high_medieval_trigger = yes
				#NOT = { has_game_rule = never_epe_fullplate_helmets }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = never_epe_fullface_helmets }					
                OR = {
                    portrait_italian_clothing_trigger = yes
                    portrait_norman_sicily_knights_clothing_trigger = yes							
                }
				
				NOR = {
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        has_government = holy_order_government
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        is_landed = no
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        exists = liege
				        liege = {
				            has_government = holy_order_government
				        }
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        OR = {
				            any_character_war = {
				                OR = {
				                    using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                    using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                }
				                is_attacker = prev
				            }
				            any_liege_or_above = {
				                faith = prev.faith
				                any_character_war = {
				                    OR = {
				                        using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                        using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                    }
				                    is_attacker = prev
				                }
				            }
				        }
				    }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	norse_high_nobles = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear
				template = norse_high_nobility
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				NAND = {
					has_trait = peasant_leader
					OR = {
						is_ruler = no
						is_leading_faction_type = peasant_faction
						AND = {
							is_ruler = yes
							is_landed = no
							OR = {
								has_government = feudal_government
								has_government = clan_government
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_duchy
							AND = {
								has_government = republic_government
								primary_title.tier > 2
							}
							AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
						}
						NOT = { AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = mercenary_government  } } # Blocked for mercenaries
						portrait_northern_clothing_trigger = yes
					}
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						OR = {
							is_ruler = no
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_barony
						}
						primary_spouse = {
							OR = {
								highest_held_title_tier = tier_duchy
								AND = {
									has_government = republic_government
									primary_title.tier > 2
								}
								AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
							}
							portrait_northern_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

						NOT = { AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = mercenary_government  } } # Blocked for mercenaries
						NOT = { has_government = republic_government }
				          portrait_dde_abbasid_clothing_trigger = yes
				          EPE_culture_era_high_medieval_trigger = yes	
				portrait_dde_abbasid_flavor_dlc_trigger = yes							  
					}
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						OR = {
							is_ruler = no
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_barony
						}
						primary_spouse = {
							OR = {
								highest_held_title_tier = tier_kingdom
								AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
							}
							NOT = { AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = mercenary_government  } } # Blocked for mercenaries
							NOT = { has_government = republic_government }
				          portrait_dde_abbasid_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
				          EPE_culture_era_high_medieval_trigger = yes	
				portrait_dde_abbasid_flavor_dlc_trigger = yes							  
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

							NOT = { has_government = republic_government }

				          EPE_culture_era_high_medieval_trigger = yes

	dde_high_abbasid_war = {
	
		dna_modifiers = {
			morph = {
				mode = add
				
				gene = gene_bs_ear_outward
				template = ear_outward_neg
				value = 1.0
			}		
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear
				template = dde_high_abbasid_war
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 101 # larger than the western war headgear
				portrait_wear_helmet_trigger = yes
			    portrait_dde_abbasid_clothing_trigger = yes
			    EPE_culture_era_high_medieval_trigger = yes	
				portrait_dde_abbasid_flavor_dlc_trigger = yes					
				
				NOR = {
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        has_government = holy_order_government
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        is_landed = no
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        exists = liege
				        liege = {
				            has_government = holy_order_government
				        }
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        OR = {
				            any_character_war = {
				                OR = {
				                    using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                    using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                }
				                is_attacker = prev
				            }
				            any_liege_or_above = {
				                faith = prev.faith
				                any_character_war = {
				                    OR = {
				                        using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                        using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                    }
				                    is_attacker = prev
				                }
				            }
				        }
				    }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	

##########Tahirid dynasty
	tahirid_dynasty_commoners = {

		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear
				template = dde_abbasid_common
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 80
				highest_held_title_tier < tier_county
				NOR = {
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						primary_spouse = {
							highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_government = republic_government
						primary_title.tier > 1
					}
					AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
				}
				portrait_tahirid_trigger = yes
				EPE_culture_era_early_medieval_trigger = yes	
			}
		}
	}

								highest_held_title_tier = tier_empire
								AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
							}
							NOT = { AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = mercenary_government  } } # Blocked for mercenaries
							NOT = { has_government = republic_government }
			            	portrait_east_african_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
						}
					}
				}

			}
		}
	}
	
	east_african_war = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			morph = {
				mode = add
				
				gene = gene_bs_ear_outward
				template = ear_outward_neg
				value = 1.0
			}		
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear
				template = east_african_war
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				portrait_wear_helmet_trigger = yes
				portrait_east_african_clothing_trigger = yes
				
				NOR = {
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        has_government = holy_order_government
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        is_landed = no
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        exists = liege
				        liege = {
				            has_government = holy_order_government
				        }
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        OR = {
				            any_character_war = {
				                OR = {
				                    using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                    using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                }
				                is_attacker = prev
				            }
				            any_liege_or_above = {
				                faith = prev.faith
				                any_character_war = {
				                    OR = {
				                        using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                        using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                    }
				                    is_attacker = prev
				                }
				            }
				        }
				    }
				}
			}
		}
	}

##Early Eastern Iranian ##

	early_eastern_iranian_commoners = {

		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear
				template = early_eastern_iranian_common
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				highest_held_title_tier < tier_county
				NOR = {
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						primary_spouse = {
							highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_government = republic_government
						primary_title.tier > 1
					}
					AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
				}
				portrait_early_eastern_iranian_trigger = yes
				portrait_non_iranian_trigger = yes				
			}
		}
	}


	early_eastern_iranian_mayors = {

				highest_held_title_tier < tier_county

				portrait_non_iranian_trigger = yes

	early_eastern_iranian_low_nobles = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear
				template = early_eastern_iranian_low_nobility
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				NAND = {
					has_trait = peasant_leader
					OR = {
						is_ruler = no
						is_leading_faction_type = peasant_faction
						AND = {
							is_ruler = yes
							is_landed = no
							OR = {
								has_government = feudal_government
								has_government = clan_government
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					AND = {
						highest_held_title_tier = tier_county
						NOR = {
							# has_dynasty = no
							AND = {
								has_government = republic_government
								primary_title.tier > 1
							}
							AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
						}
						portrait_early_eastern_iranian_trigger = yes
						portrait_non_iranian_trigger = yes						
					}
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						OR = {
							is_ruler = no
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_barony
						}
						primary_spouse = {
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_county
							NOR = {
								# has_dynasty = no
								AND = {
									has_government = republic_government
									primary_title.tier > 1
								}
								AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
							}
					    portrait_early_eastern_iranian_spouse_trigger = yes	
						portrait_non_iranian_trigger = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

###Early non-Islamic war helmet closed face	
	early_eastern_iranian_war_closed = {
		dna_modifiers = {
		
			morph = {
				mode = add
				
				gene = gene_bs_ear_outward
				template = ear_outward_neg
				value = 1.0
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify
				gene = gene_chin_forward
				template = chin_forward_neg
				value = -1.0
		
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify
				gene = gene_jaw_forward
				template = jaw_forward_pos
				value = -1.0
			}			
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply				
				gene = gene_bs_nose_forward
				template = nose_forward_neg				
				value = 1.0
			}		
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear_2
				template = early_eastern_iranian_war_closed
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100				
				portrait_wear_helmet_trigger = yes
				portrait_early_eastern_iranian_trigger = yes	
				portrait_non_iranian_trigger = yes					
				NOT = { has_game_rule = never_epe_fullface_helmets }						
				
				NOR = {
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        has_government = holy_order_government
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        is_landed = no
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        exists = liege
				        liege = {
				            has_government = holy_order_government
				        }
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        OR = {
				            any_character_war = {
				                OR = {
				                    using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                    using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                }
				                is_attacker = prev
				            }
				            any_liege_or_above = {
				                faith = prev.faith
				                any_character_war = {
				                    OR = {
				                        using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                        using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                    }
				                    is_attacker = prev
				                }
				            }
				        }
				    }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	early_islamic_iranian_imperial = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear
				template = early_islamic_iranian_imperial
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				NAND = {
					has_trait = peasant_leader
					OR = {
						is_ruler = no
						is_leading_faction_type = peasant_faction
						AND = {
							is_ruler = yes
							is_landed = no
							OR = {
								has_government = feudal_government
								has_government = clan_government
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_empire
							AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
						}
						NOT = { AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = mercenary_government  } } # Blocked for mercenaries
						NOT = { has_government = republic_government }
				portrait_iranian_clothing_trigger = yes
				portrait_islamic_iranian_trigger = yes
				EPE_culture_era_early_medieval_trigger = yes		
					}
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						OR = {
							is_ruler = no
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_barony
						}
						primary_spouse = {
							OR = {
								highest_held_title_tier = tier_empire
								AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
							}
							NOT = { AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = mercenary_government  } } # Blocked for mercenaries
							NOT = { has_government = republic_government }
				portrait_iranian_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
				portrait_islamic_iranian_trigger = yes
				EPE_culture_era_early_medieval_trigger = yes			
						}
					}
				}

			}
		}
	}	
	
	early_islamic_iranian_war = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			morph = {
				mode = add
				
				gene = gene_bs_ear_outward
				template = ear_outward_neg
				value = 1.0
			}		
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear
				template = early_islamic_iranian_war
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100 # larger than the western war headgear
				portrait_wear_helmet_trigger = yes
				portrait_iranian_clothing_trigger = yes
				portrait_islamic_iranian_trigger = yes
				EPE_culture_era_early_medieval_trigger = yes			
				
				NOR = {
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        has_government = holy_order_government
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        is_landed = no
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        exists = liege
				        liege = {
				            has_government = holy_order_government
				        }
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        OR = {
				            any_character_war = {
				                OR = {
				                    using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                    using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                }
				                is_attacker = prev
				            }
				            any_liege_or_above = {
				                faith = prev.faith
				                any_character_war = {
				                    OR = {
				                        using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                        using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                    }
				                    is_attacker = prev
				                }
				            }
				        }
				    }
				}
			}
		}
	}	
###Early Islamic war helmet closed face	
	early_islamic_iranian_war_closed = {
		dna_modifiers = {
		
			morph = {
				mode = add
				
				gene = gene_bs_ear_outward
				template = ear_outward_neg
				value = 1.0
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify
				gene = gene_chin_forward
				template = chin_forward_neg
				value = -1.0
		
			}
			morph = {
				mode = modify
				gene = gene_jaw_forward
				template = jaw_forward_pos
				value = -1.0
			}			
			morph = {
				mode = modify_multiply				
				gene = gene_bs_nose_forward
				template = nose_forward_neg				
				value = 1.0
			}		
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear
				template = early_islamic_iranian_war_closed
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100				
				portrait_wear_helmet_trigger = yes
				portrait_iranian_clothing_trigger = yes
				portrait_islamic_iranian_trigger = yes
				EPE_culture_era_early_medieval_trigger = yes	
				NOT = { has_game_rule = never_epe_fullface_helmets }						
				
				NOR = {
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        has_government = holy_order_government
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        is_landed = no
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        exists = liege
				        liege = {
				            has_government = holy_order_government
				        }
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        OR = {
				            any_character_war = {
				                OR = {
				                    using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                    using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                }
				                is_attacker = prev
				            }
				            any_liege_or_above = {
				                faith = prev.faith
				                any_character_war = {
				                    OR = {
				                        using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                        using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                    }
				                    is_attacker = prev
				                }
				            }
				        }
				    }
				}
			}
		}
	}	
	


##########Shahi dynasty
	shahi_dynasty_commoners = {

		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear
				template = indian_common
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				highest_held_title_tier < tier_county
				NOR = {
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						primary_spouse = {
							highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_government = republic_government
						primary_title.tier > 1
					}
					AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
				}
				portrait_shahi_trigger = yes
			}
		}
	}

						exists = primary_spouse
						OR = {
							is_ruler = no
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_barony
						}
						primary_spouse = {
							OR = {
								highest_held_title_tier = tier_kingdom
								AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
							}
							NOT = { AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = mercenary_government  } } # Blocked for mercenaries
							NOT = { has_government = republic_government }
						portrait_northern_slav_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	northern_slav_war = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			morph = {
				mode = add
				
				gene = gene_bs_ear_outward
				template = ear_outward_neg
				value = 1.0
			}		
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear
				template = northern_slav_war
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 101 # larger than the western war headgear
				portrait_wear_helmet_trigger = yes
				portrait_northern_slav_clothing_trigger = yes
				
				NOR = {
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        has_government = holy_order_government
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        is_landed = no
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        exists = liege
				        liege = {
				            has_government = holy_order_government
				        }
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        OR = {
				            any_character_war = {
				                OR = {
				                    using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                    using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                }
				                is_attacker = prev
				            }
				            any_liege_or_above = {
				                faith = prev.faith
				                any_character_war = {
				                    OR = {
				                        using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                        using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                    }
				                    is_attacker = prev
				                }
				            }
				        }
				    }
				}
			}
		}
	}			
	
###northern slav non dlc version
	northern_slav_non_dlc_commoners = {

		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear
				template = western_common
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 80
				has_trait = peasant_leader
				OR = {
					is_ruler = no
					is_leading_faction_type = peasant_faction
					AND = {
						is_ruler = yes
						is_landed = no
						OR = {
							has_government = feudal_government
							has_government = clan_government
						}
					}
				}
						portrait_northern_slav_clothing_trigger = yes
                        NOT = { portrait_norse_flavor_dlc_trigger = yes } 	
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				highest_held_title_tier < tier_county
				NOR = {
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						primary_spouse = {
							highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_government = republic_government
						primary_title.tier > 1
					}
					AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
				}
						portrait_northern_slav_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
                        NOT = { portrait_norse_flavor_dlc_trigger = yes } 	
			}
		}
	}

							AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
						}
						portrait_cuman_clothing_trigger = yes
						EPE_culture_era_high_medieval_trigger = yes	
					}
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						OR = {
							is_ruler = no
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_barony
						}
						primary_spouse = {
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_county
							NOR = {
								# has_dynasty = no
								AND = {
									has_government = republic_government
									primary_title.tier > 1
								}
								AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
							}
							portrait_cuman_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
							EPE_culture_era_high_medieval_trigger = yes	
						}
					}
				}

			}
		}
	}

	cuman_high_late_war = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			morph = {
				mode = add
				
				gene = gene_bs_ear_outward
				template = ear_outward_neg
				value = 1.0
			}		
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear
				template = cuman_high_late_war
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				portrait_wear_helmet_trigger = yes
				portrait_cuman_clothing_trigger = yes
				EPE_culture_era_high_medieval_trigger = yes		
				
				NOR = {
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        has_government = holy_order_government
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        is_landed = no
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        exists = liege
				        liege = {
				            has_government = holy_order_government
				        }
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        OR = {
				            any_character_war = {
				                OR = {
				                    using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                    using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                }
				                is_attacker = prev
				            }
				            any_liege_or_above = {
				                faith = prev.faith
				                any_character_war = {
				                    OR = {
				                        using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                        using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                    }
				                    is_attacker = prev
				                }
				            }
				        }
				    }
				}
			}
		}
	}

							AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
						}
						NOT = { AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = mercenary_government  } } # Blocked for mercenaries
						NOT = { has_government = republic_government }
				portrait_balto_finnic_clothing_trigger = yes				
				portrait_norse_flavor_dlc_trigger = yes

					AND = {

							is_ruler = no
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_barony
						}
						primary_spouse = {
							OR = {

							}

	balto_finnic_war = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			morph = {
				mode = add
				
				gene = gene_bs_ear_outward
				template = ear_outward_neg
				value = 1.0
			}		
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear
				template = balto_finnic_war
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 101 # larger than the western war headgear
				portrait_wear_helmet_trigger = yes				
				portrait_balto_finnic_clothing_trigger = yes				
				
				NOR = {
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        has_government = holy_order_government
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        is_landed = no
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        exists = liege
				        liege = {
				            has_government = holy_order_government
				        }
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        OR = {
				            any_character_war = {
				                OR = {
				                    using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                    using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                }
				                is_attacker = prev
				            }
				            any_liege_or_above = {
				                faith = prev.faith
				                any_character_war = {
				                    OR = {
				                        using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                        using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                    }
				                    is_attacker = prev
				                }
				            }
				        }
				    }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	iberia_commoners = {

			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear
				template = iberia_common
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				highest_held_title_tier < tier_county
				NOR = {
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						primary_spouse = {
							highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_government = republic_government
						primary_title.tier > 1
					}
					AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
				}
				portrait_iberia_clothing_trigger = yes
				portrait_iberia_trigger = yes	
		###High medieval headgears		
				OR = {
				EPE_culture_era_high_medieval_trigger = yes	##High to late era			
				current_date >= 1026.1.1	##early era				
				}				
			}
		}
	}
