							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_kingdom
							AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
						}
						NOT = { AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = mercenary_government  } } # Blocked for mercenaries
						NOT = { has_government = republic_government }
						portrait_maghreb_clothing_trigger = yes
					}
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						OR = {
							is_ruler = no
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_barony
						}
						primary_spouse = {
							OR = {
								highest_held_title_tier = tier_kingdom
								AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
							}
							NOT = { AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = mercenary_government  } } # Blocked for mercenaries
							NOT = { has_government = republic_government }
							portrait_maghreb_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

				portrait_maghreb_clothing_trigger = yes

				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        has_government = holy_order_government
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        is_landed = no
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        exists = liege
				        liege = {
				            has_government = holy_order_government
				        }
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        OR = {
				            any_character_war = {
				                OR = {
				                    using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                    using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                }
				                is_attacker = prev
				            }
				            any_liege_or_above = {
				                faith = prev.faith
				                any_character_war = {
				                    OR = {
				                        using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                        using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                    }
				                    is_attacker = prev
				                }
				            }
				        }
				    }
				}
			}
		}
	}

						}

	anglo_saxon_imperial = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear
				template = anglo_saxon_imperial
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				NAND = {
					has_trait = peasant_leader
					OR = {
						is_ruler = no
						is_leading_faction_type = peasant_faction
						AND = {
							is_ruler = yes
							is_landed = no
							OR = {
								has_government = feudal_government
								has_government = clan_government
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_empire
							AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
						}
						NOT = { AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = mercenary_government  } } # Blocked for mercenaries
						NOT = { has_government = republic_government }
						portrait_anglo_saxon_clothing_trigger = yes
					}
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						OR = {
							is_ruler = no
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_barony
						}
						primary_spouse = {
							OR = {
								highest_held_title_tier = tier_empire
								AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
							}
							NOT = { AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = mercenary_government  } } # Blocked for mercenaries
							NOT = { has_government = republic_government }

	anglo_saxon_war = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			morph = {
				mode = add
				
				gene = gene_bs_ear_outward
				template = ear_outward_neg
				value = 1.0
			}		
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear
				template = anglo_saxon_war
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				portrait_wear_helmet_trigger = yes
				portrait_anglo_saxon_clothing_trigger = yes
				EPE_armor_era_early_medieval_trigger = yes																
				NOR = {
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        has_government = holy_order_government
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        is_landed = no
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        exists = liege
				        liege = {
				            has_government = holy_order_government
				        }
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        OR = {
				            any_character_war = {
				                OR = {
				                    using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                    using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                }
				                is_attacker = prev
				            }
				            any_liege_or_above = {
				                faith = prev.faith
				                any_character_war = {
				                    OR = {
				                        using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                        using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                    }
				                    is_attacker = prev
				                }
				            }
				        }
				    }
				}
			}
		}
	}

				NOR = {
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						primary_spouse = {
							highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_government = republic_government
						primary_title.tier > 1
					}
					AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
				}
				portrait_polish_clothing_trigger = yes
		###High medieval headgears		
				OR = {
				EPE_culture_era_high_medieval_trigger = yes	##High to late era			
				current_date >= 1026.1.1	##early era				
				}				
			}
		}

		###High medieval headgears		
				OR = {
				EPE_culture_era_high_medieval_trigger = yes	##High to late era			
				current_date >= 1026.1.1	##early era				
				}							
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_empire
							AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
						}
						NOT = { AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = mercenary_government  } } # Blocked for mercenaries
						NOT = { has_government = republic_government }
						portrait_west_slav_clothing_trigger = yes
		###High medieval headgears		
				OR = {
				EPE_culture_era_high_medieval_trigger = yes	##High to late era			
				current_date >= 1026.1.1	##early era				
				}						
					}

						}
						primary_spouse = {
							OR = {
								highest_held_title_tier = tier_empire
								AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
							}
							NOT = { AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = mercenary_government  } } # Blocked for mercenaries
							NOT = { has_government = republic_government }
							portrait_west_slav_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
		###High medieval headgears		
				OR = {
				EPE_culture_era_high_medieval_trigger = yes	##High to late era			
				current_date >= 1026.1.1	##early era

	west_slav_war = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			morph = {
				mode = add
				
				gene = gene_bs_ear_outward
				template = ear_outward_neg
				value = 1.0
			}		
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear
				template = west_slav_war
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				portrait_wear_helmet_trigger = yes
				portrait_west_slav_clothing_trigger = yes
			 OR = {
					EPE_armor_era_tribal_medieval_trigger = yes
				    EPE_armor_era_early_medieval_trigger = yes												
				}				
				NOR = {
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        has_government = holy_order_government
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        is_landed = no
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        exists = liege
				        liege = {
				            has_government = holy_order_government
				        }
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        OR = {
				            any_character_war = {
				                OR = {
				                    using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                    using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                }
				                is_attacker = prev
				            }
				            any_liege_or_above = {
				                faith = prev.faith
				                any_character_war = {
				                    OR = {
				                        using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                        using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                    }
				                    is_attacker = prev
				                }
				            }
				        }
				    }
				}
			}
		}
	}

						portrait_kirghiz_clothing_trigger = yes
					}
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						OR = {
							is_ruler = no
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_barony
						}
						primary_spouse = {
							OR = {
								highest_held_title_tier = tier_kingdom
								AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
							}
							NOT = { AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = mercenary_government  } } # Blocked for mercenaries
							NOT = { has_government = republic_government }
							portrait_kirghiz_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	kirghiz_imperial = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear
				template = kirghiz_imperial
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				NAND = {
					has_trait = peasant_leader
					OR = {
						is_ruler = no
						is_leading_faction_type = peasant_faction
						AND = {
							is_ruler = yes
							is_landed = no
							OR = {
								has_government = feudal_government
								has_government = clan_government
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_empire
							AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
						}
						NOT = { AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = mercenary_government  } } # Blocked for mercenaries
						NOT = { has_government = republic_government }
						portrait_kirghiz_clothing_trigger = yes
					}
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						OR = {
							is_ruler = no
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_barony
						}
						primary_spouse = {
							OR = {
								highest_held_title_tier = tier_empire
								AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
							}
							NOT = { AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = mercenary_government  } } # Blocked for mercenaries
							NOT = { has_government = republic_government }
							portrait_kirghiz_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
						}
					}
				}

			}
		}
	}


	kirghiz_war = {

				portrait_kirghiz_clothing_trigger = yes

				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        has_government = holy_order_government
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        is_landed = no
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        exists = liege
				        liege = {
				            has_government = holy_order_government
				        }
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        OR = {
				            any_character_war = {
				                OR = {
				                    using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                    using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                }
				                is_attacker = prev
				            }
				            any_liege_or_above = {
				                faith = prev.faith
				                any_character_war = {
				                    OR = {
				                        using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                        using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                    }
				                    is_attacker = prev
				                }
				            }
				        }
				    }
				}
			}
		}
	}

					portrait_western_clothing_trigger = yes
				    portrait_dde_hre_clothing_trigger = yes							
					portrait_french_clothing_trigger = yes
					portrait_italian_clothing_trigger = yes			
								AND = {
				    portrait_iberia_clothing_trigger = yes	
						portrait_iberia_trigger = yes				
								}
			        portrait_hungarian_clothing_trigger = yes	
				    portrait_polish_clothing_trigger = yes
				    portrait_german_clothing_trigger = yes					
			
				}
				
				NOR = {
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        has_government = holy_order_government
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        is_landed = no
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        exists = liege
				        liege = {
				            has_government = holy_order_government
				        }
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        OR = {
				            any_character_war = {
				                OR = {
				                    using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                    using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                }
				                is_attacker = prev
				            }
				            any_liege_or_above = {
				                faith = prev.faith
				                any_character_war = {
				                    OR = {
				                        using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                        using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                    }
				                    is_attacker = prev
				                }
				            }
				        }
				    }
				}
			}
		}
	}

				EPE_culture_era_early_medieval_trigger = yes	
						}
					}
				}

			}
		}
	}

	non_dlc_abbasid_war = {
	
		dna_modifiers = {
			morph = {
				mode = add
				
				gene = gene_bs_ear_outward
				template = ear_outward_neg
				value = 1.0
			}		
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear_2
				template = non_dlc_abbasid_war
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 101 # slightly higher than mena
				OR = { # This helmet is really fancy & gilded - it's nothing for commoners. We allow Dukes+ to use it sometimes, just because it suits them!
					AND = {
						has_council_position = councillor_marshal
						OR = {
							is_landed = no
							primary_title.tier >= tier_duchy
						}
					}
					AND = {
						is_commanding_army = yes
						AND = {
							exists = primary_title
							primary_title.tier >= tier_duchy
						}
					}
				}
				portrait_dde_abbasid_clothing_trigger = yes	
                NOT = { portrait_dde_abbasid_flavor_dlc_trigger = yes } 	
				EPE_culture_era_early_medieval_trigger = yes	
				
				NOR = {
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        has_government = holy_order_government
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        is_landed = no
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        exists = liege
				        liege = {
				            has_government = holy_order_government
				        }
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        OR = {
				            any_character_war = {
				                OR = {
				                    using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                    using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                }
				                is_attacker = prev
				            }
				            any_liege_or_above = {
				                faith = prev.faith
				                any_character_war = {
				                    OR = {
				                        using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                        using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                    }
				                    is_attacker = prev
				                }
				            }
				        }
				    }
					AND = {
						has_trait = peasant_leader
						OR = {
							is_ruler = no
							is_leading_faction_type = peasant_faction
							AND = {
								is_ruler = yes
								is_landed = no
								OR = {
									has_government = feudal_government
									has_government = clan_government
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

						}
					}
				}
				portrait_sahelian_clothing_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				highest_held_title_tier < tier_county
				NOR = {
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						primary_spouse = {
							highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_government = republic_government
						primary_title.tier > 1
					}
					AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
				}
				portrait_sahelian_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
			}
		}
	}

	sahelian_war = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			morph = {
				mode = add
				
				gene = gene_bs_ear_outward
				template = ear_outward_neg
				value = 1.0
			}		
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear_2
				template = sahelian_war
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				portrait_wear_helmet_trigger = yes
				portrait_sahelian_clothing_trigger = yes
				
				NOR = {
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        has_government = holy_order_government
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        is_landed = no
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        exists = liege
				        liege = {
				            has_government = holy_order_government
				        }
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        OR = {
				            any_character_war = {
				                OR = {
				                    using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                    using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                }
				                is_attacker = prev
				            }
				            any_liege_or_above = {
				                faith = prev.faith
				                any_character_war = {
				                    OR = {
				                        using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                        using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                    }
				                    is_attacker = prev
				                }
				            }
				        }
				    }
				}
			}
		}
	}

####Anglo-Saxon war helmets tribal era

	tribal_era_anglo_saxon_war = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			morph = {
				mode = add
				
				gene = gene_bs_ear_outward
				template = ear_outward_neg
				value = 1.0
			}			
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear_2
				template = tribal_era_anglo_saxon_war
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear
				template = no_headgear
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}			
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				portrait_wear_helmet_trigger = yes
				EPE_armor_era_tribal_medieval_trigger = yes						
			 OR = {
				    portrait_anglo_saxon_clothing_trigger = yes					
				}
				
				NOR = {
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        has_government = holy_order_government
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        is_landed = no
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        exists = liege
				        liege = {
				            has_government = holy_order_government
				        }
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        OR = {
				            any_character_war = {
				                OR = {
				                    using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                    using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                }
				                is_attacker = prev
				            }
				            any_liege_or_above = {
				                faith = prev.faith
				                any_character_war = {
				                    OR = {
				                        using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                        using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                    }
				                    is_attacker = prev
				                }
				            }
				        }
				    }
				}
			}
		}
	}

									primary_title.tier > 1
								}
								AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
							}
							portrait_bulgarian_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	bulgarian_high_nobles = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear_2
				template = bulgarian_high_nobility
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				NAND = {
					has_trait = peasant_leader
					OR = {
						is_ruler = no
						is_leading_faction_type = peasant_faction
						AND = {
							is_ruler = yes
							is_landed = no
							OR = {
								has_government = feudal_government
								has_government = clan_government
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_duchy
							AND = {
								has_government = republic_government
								primary_title.tier > 2
							}
							AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
						}
						NOT = { AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = mercenary_government  } } # Blocked for mercenaries
						portrait_bulgarian_clothing_trigger = yes
					}
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						OR = {
							is_ruler = no
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_barony
						}
						primary_spouse = {
							OR = {
								highest_held_title_tier = tier_duchy
								AND = {
									has_government = republic_government
									primary_title.tier > 2
								}
								AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
							}
							portrait_bulgarian_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	bulgarian_war = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			morph = {
				mode = add
				
				gene = gene_bs_ear_outward
				template = ear_outward_neg
				value = 1.0
			}		
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear_2
				template = bulgarian_war
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 101 # larger than the western war headgear
				portrait_wear_helmet_trigger = yes
				portrait_bulgarian_clothing_trigger = yes
				
				NOR = {
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        has_government = holy_order_government
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        is_landed = no
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        exists = liege
				        liege = {
				            has_government = holy_order_government
				        }
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        OR = {
				            any_character_war = {
				                OR = {
				                    using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                    using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                }
				                is_attacker = prev
				            }
				            any_liege_or_above = {
				                faith = prev.faith
				                any_character_war = {
				                    OR = {
				                        using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                        using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                    }
				                    is_attacker = prev
				                }
				            }
				        }
				    }
				}
			}
		}
	}	
	
## armenian ##


	armenian_commoners = {

		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear_2
				template = armenian_common
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				highest_held_title_tier < tier_county
				NOR = {
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						primary_spouse = {
							highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_government = republic_government
						primary_title.tier > 1
					}
					AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
				}
				portrait_armenian_clothing_trigger = yes
			}
		}
	}

								AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
							}
							NOT = { AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = mercenary_government  } } # Blocked for mercenaries
							NOT = { has_government = republic_government }
							portrait_south_slav_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}	
	
	
	south_slav_imperial = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear_2
				template = south_slav_imperial
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}			
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				NAND = {
					has_trait = peasant_leader
					OR = {
						is_ruler = no
						is_leading_faction_type = peasant_faction
						AND = {
							is_ruler = yes
							is_landed = no
							OR = {
								has_government = feudal_government
								has_government = clan_government
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_empire
							AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
						}
						NOT = { AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = mercenary_government  } } # Blocked for mercenaries
						NOT = { has_government = republic_government }
				        portrait_south_slav_clothing_trigger = yes
					}
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						OR = {
							is_ruler = no
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_barony
						}
						primary_spouse = {
							OR = {
								highest_held_title_tier = tier_empire
								AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
							}
							NOT = { AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = mercenary_government  } } # Blocked for mercenaries
							NOT = { has_government = republic_government }
			            	portrait_south_slav_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
						}
					}
				}

			}
		}
	}	
	
	south_slav_war = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			morph = {
				mode = add
				
				gene = gene_bs_ear_outward
				template = ear_outward_neg
				value = 1.0
			}		
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear_2
				template = south_slav_war
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 101 # larger than the western war headgear
				portrait_wear_helmet_trigger = yes
				portrait_south_slav_clothing_trigger = yes
				
				NOR = {
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        has_government = holy_order_government
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        is_landed = no
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        exists = liege
				        liege = {
				            has_government = holy_order_government
				        }
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        OR = {
				            any_character_war = {
				                OR = {
				                    using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                    using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                }
				                is_attacker = prev
				            }
				            any_liege_or_above = {
				                faith = prev.faith
				                any_character_war = {
				                    OR = {
				                        using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                        using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                    }
				                    is_attacker = prev
				                }
				            }
				        }
				    }
				}
			}
		}
	}	
	


## merovingian ##

	merovingian_commoners = {

		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear_2
				template = merovingian_common
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 89
				highest_held_title_tier < tier_county
				NOR = {
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						primary_spouse = {
							highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_government = republic_government
						primary_title.tier > 1
					}
					AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
				}
				portrait_merovingian_clothing_trigger = yes
			}
		}
	}

	karling_commoners = {

		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear_2
				template = karling_common
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				highest_held_title_tier < tier_county
				NOR = {
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						primary_spouse = {
							highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_government = republic_government
						primary_title.tier > 1
					}
					AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
				}
				OR = {
					portrait_german_clothing_trigger = yes
				    portrait_dde_hre_clothing_trigger = yes	
					portrait_french_clothing_trigger = yes							
				}
		###tribal medieval headgears		
			OR = {
				EPE_armor_era_tribal_medieval_trigger = yes		
				current_date <= 1026.1.1	##early era				
				}	
			}
		}
	}

				}		
					}

						}
						primary_spouse = {
							OR = {
								highest_held_title_tier = tier_empire

			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				NAND = {
					has_trait = peasant_leader
					OR = {
						is_ruler = no
						is_leading_faction_type = peasant_faction
						AND = {
							is_ruler = yes
							is_landed = no
							OR = {
								has_government = feudal_government
								has_government = clan_government
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_duchy
							AND = {
								has_government = republic_government
								primary_title.tier > 2
							}
							AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
						}
						NOT = { AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = mercenary_government  } } # Blocked for mercenaries
							portrait_bedouin_clothing_trigger = yes		
					}
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						OR = {
							is_ruler = no
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_barony
						}
						primary_spouse = {
							OR = {
								highest_held_title_tier = tier_duchy
								AND = {
									has_government = republic_government
									primary_title.tier > 2
								}
								AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
							}
							portrait_bedouin_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes	
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	bedouin_war = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			morph = {
				mode = add
				
				gene = gene_bs_ear_outward
				template = ear_outward_neg
				value = 1.0
			}		
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear_2
				template = bedouin_war
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				portrait_wear_helmet_trigger = yes
				portrait_bedouin_clothing_trigger = yes
				
				NOR = {
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        has_government = holy_order_government
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        is_landed = no
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        exists = liege
				        liege = {
				            has_government = holy_order_government
				        }
				    }
				    AND = {
				        religion = religion:christianity_religion
				        portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
				        OR = {
				            any_character_war = {
				                OR = {
				                    using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                    using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                }
				                is_attacker = prev
				            }
				            any_liege_or_above = {
				                faith = prev.faith
				                any_character_war = {
				                    OR = {
				                        using_cb = undirected_great_holy_war
				                        using_cb = directed_great_holy_war
				                    }
				                    is_attacker = prev
				                }
				            }
				        }
				    }
				}
			}
		}
	}

							highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_government = republic_government
						primary_title.tier > 1
					}
					AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
				}
				portrait_tibetan_clothing_trigger = yes
			}
		}

	early_western_commoners = {

		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear_2
				template = early_western_common
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				highest_held_title_tier < tier_county
				NOR = {
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						primary_spouse = {
							highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_government = republic_government
						primary_title.tier > 1
					}
					AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
				}
			 OR = {
					portrait_western_clothing_trigger = yes
			        portrait_hungarian_clothing_trigger = yes	
				    portrait_polish_clothing_trigger = yes				
				    portrait_west_slav_clothing_trigger = yes					
				}
		###tribal medieval headgears		
			OR = {
				EPE_armor_era_tribal_medieval_trigger = yes		
				current_date <= 1026.1.1	##early era				
				}	
			}
		}
	}

	early_western_high_nobles = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear_2
				template = early_western_high_nobility
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				NAND = {
					has_trait = peasant_leader
					OR = {
						is_ruler = no
						is_leading_faction_type = peasant_faction
						AND = {
							is_ruler = yes
							is_landed = no
							OR = {
								has_government = feudal_government
								has_government = clan_government
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_duchy
							AND = {
								has_government = republic_government
								primary_title.tier > 2
							}
							AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
						}
						NOT = { AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = mercenary_government  } } # Blocked for mercenaries
			 OR = {
					portrait_western_clothing_trigger = yes
			        portrait_hungarian_clothing_trigger = yes	
				    portrait_polish_clothing_trigger = yes				
				    portrait_west_slav_clothing_trigger = yes					
				}
		###tribal medieval headgears		
			OR = {
				EPE_armor_era_tribal_medieval_trigger = yes		
				current_date <= 1026.1.1	##early era				
				}
					}
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						OR = {
							is_ruler = no
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_barony
						}
						primary_spouse = {
							OR = {
								highest_held_title_tier = tier_duchy
								AND = {
									has_government = republic_government
									primary_title.tier > 2
								}
								AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
							}
			 OR = {
					portrait_western_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
			        portrait_hungarian_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes	
				    portrait_polish_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes				
				    portrait_west_slav_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes					
				}
		###tribal medieval headgears		
			OR = {
				EPE_armor_era_tribal_medieval_trigger = yes		
				current_date <= 1026.1.1	##early era				
				}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	early_italian_commoners = {

		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear_2
				template = early_italian_common
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				highest_held_title_tier < tier_county
				NOR = {
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						primary_spouse = {
							highest_held_title_tier > tier_county
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_government = republic_government
						primary_title.tier > 1
					}
					AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
				}
			 OR = {
						portrait_italian_clothing_trigger = yes				
				}
		###tribal medieval headgears		
			OR = {
				EPE_armor_era_tribal_medieval_trigger = yes		
				current_date <= 1026.1.1	##early era				
				}	
			}
		}
	}

						NOR = {
							# has_dynasty = no
							AND = {
								has_government = republic_government
								primary_title.tier > 1
							}
							AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
						}
				portrait_iberia_clothing_trigger = yes
			    portrait_iberia_trigger = yes	
		###tribal medieval headgears		
			OR = {
				EPE_armor_era_tribal_medieval_trigger = yes		
				current_date <= 1026.1.1	##early era				
				}
					}
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						OR = {
							is_ruler = no
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_barony
						}
						primary_spouse = {
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_county
							NOR = {
								# has_dynasty = no
								AND = {
									has_government = republic_government
									primary_title.tier > 1
								}
								AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
							}
							portrait_iberia_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
						    portrait_iberia_trigger = yes	
		###tribal medieval headgears		
			OR = {
				EPE_armor_era_tribal_medieval_trigger = yes		
				current_date <= 1026.1.1	##early era				
				}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	visigoth_high_nobles = {
		dna_modifiers = {
			accessory = {
				mode = add
				gene = headgear_2
				template = visigoth_high_nobility
				range = { 0 1 } # For the randomness to work correctly
			}
		}	
		weight = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				NAND = {
					has_trait = peasant_leader
					OR = {
						is_ruler = no
						is_leading_faction_type = peasant_faction
						AND = {
							is_ruler = yes
							is_landed = no
							OR = {
								has_government = feudal_government
								has_government = clan_government
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_duchy
							AND = {
								has_government = republic_government
								primary_title.tier > 2
							}
							AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
						}
						NOT = { AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = mercenary_government  } } # Blocked for mercenaries
				portrait_iberia_clothing_trigger = yes
			    portrait_iberia_trigger = yes	
		###tribal medieval headgears		
			OR = {
				EPE_armor_era_tribal_medieval_trigger = yes		
				current_date <= 1026.1.1	##early era				
				}
					}
					AND = {
						exists = primary_spouse
						OR = {
							is_ruler = no
							highest_held_title_tier = tier_barony
						}
						primary_spouse = {
							OR = {
								highest_held_title_tier = tier_duchy
								AND = {
									has_government = republic_government
									primary_title.tier > 2
								}
								AND = { is_ruler = yes has_government = theocracy_government }
							}
							portrait_iberia_clothing_spouse_trigger = yes
						    portrait_iberia_trigger = yes	
		###tribal medieval headgears		
			OR = {
				EPE_armor_era_tribal_medieval_trigger = yes		
				current_date <= 1026.1.1	##early era				
				}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

				any_parent = { highest_held_title_tier = tier_kingdom }
				any_parent = { highest_held_title_tier = tier_empire }					
						}

				}

				is_landed = no

			}
